 namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa  
 sutta nipāta  
 i  uragavagga  
    uragasutta  
    yo  uppatitaṃ vineti kodhaṃ 
 visataṃ  sappavisaṃ va osadhehi  
 so bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ 
 urago jiṇṇam iva tacaṃ purāṇaṃ     sn i        
    yo rāgam udacchidā asesa 
 bhisapupphaṃ va saroruhaṃ vigayha  
 so bhikkhu           sn i        
    yo taṇham udacchidā asesaṃ 
 saritaṃ sīghasaraṃ visosayitvā   
 so bhikkhu          sn i        
    yo mānam udabbadhī asesaṃ 
 naḷasetuṃ va sudubbalaṃ mahogho  
 so bhikkhu          sn i        
  f        yo najjhagamā bhavesu sāraṃ 
 vicinaṃ puppham iva udumbaresu  
 so bhikkhu          sn i        
    yass  antarato na santi kopa 
 itibhavābhavatañ ca vītivatto  
 so bhikkhu          sn i        
  
                                                                            so pj  bai  ckb yo ve  dhp        
   bai visaṭaṃ  
   ck writes the text in full throughout  
   ck visesayitvā  cb visesayitvā corr  to visosayitvā

   uragaragga 
    yassa vitakkā vidhūpitā  
 ajjhattaṃ suvikappitā asesā  
 so bhikkhu          sn i        
    yo nāccasārī  na paccasārī  
 sabbaṃ accagamā  imaṃ papañcaṃ  
 so bhikkhu          sn i        
    yo nāccasārī na paccasārī 
  sabbam vitatham idan  ti ñatvā loke  
 so bhikkhu          sn i        
     yo nāccasārī na paccasārī 
  sabbaṃ vitatham idan  ti vītalobho  
 so bhikkhu          sn i         
     yo nāccasārī na paccasārī 
  sabbaṃ vitatham idan  ti vītarāgo  
 so bhikkhu          sn i         
     yo nāccasārī na paccasārī 
  sabbaṃ vitatham idan  ti vītadoso  
 so bhikkhu          sn i         
     yo nāccasārī na paccasārī 
  sabbaṃ vitatham idan  ti vītamoho  
 so bhikkhu          sn i         
     yassānusayā  na santi keci  
 mūlā akusalā samūhatāse

 oraṃ āgamanāya paccayāse

     yassa vanathajā na santi keci 
 vinibandhāya bhavāya hetukappā  
 so bhikkhu          sn i

 uragavagga   
     yo nīvaraṇe pahāya pañca 
 anigho  tiṇṇakathaṃkatho visallo  
 so bhikkhu jahāti orapāraṃ 
 urago jiṇṇam iva tacaṃ purāṇan ti    sn i         
 uragasuttaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
    dhaniyasutta  
      pakkodano duddhakhīro  ham asmi 
 iti dhaniyo gopo 
 anutīre mahiyā samānavāso  
 channā kuṭi  āhito gini   atha ce patthayasī   pavassa davassa deva      sn i        
      akkodhano vigatakhīlo  ham asmi 
 iti bhagavā 
 anutīre mahiy  ekarattivāso  
 vivaṭā kuṭi  nibbuto gini   atha ce patthayasī   pavassa deva      sn i        
      andhakamakasā na vijjare  
 iti dhaniyo gopo 
 kacche  rūḷhatiṇe caranti gāvo  
 vuṭṭhim pi saheyyuṃ āgataṃ   atha ce patthayasī   pavassa deva      sn i        
      baddhā hi bhisī  susaṃkhatā   
 iti bhagavā 
 tiṇṇo pāragato  vineyya oghaṃ  
  f     attho bhisiyā na vijjati   atha ce patthayasī   pavassa deva      sn i

      gopī  mama assavā alolā 
 iti dhaniyo gopo 
 dīgharattaṃ  saṃvāsiyā manāpā  
 tassā na suṇāmi kiñci pāpaṃ   atha ce   pe       sn i        
      cittaṃ mama assavaṃ vimuttaṃ 
 iti bhagavā

 pāpam  pana me na vijjati   atha ce           sn i        
      attavetanabhato  ham asmi  
 iti dhaniyo gopo 
 puttā ca me  samāniyā arogā   
 tesaṃ na suṇāmi kiñci pāpaṃ   atha ce           sn i        
      nāhaṃ bhatako  smi kassaci  
 iti bhagavā  
 nibbitthena carāmi sabbaloke  
 attho bhatiyā  na vijjati   atha ce           sn i        
      atthi vasā  atthi dhenupā

  f     na hi sakkhiti  dhenupā pi chettuṃ    atha ce           sn i         
      usabho r iva chetva  bandhanāni 
 iti bhagavā 
 nāgo pūtilataṃ va dālayitvā  
 nāhaṃ puna upessaṃ  gabbhaseyyaṃ   atha ce patthayasī  pavassa deva      sn i         
     ninnañ ca thalañ ca pūrayanto 
 mahāmegho pāvassi tāvad eva  
 sutvā devassa vassato 
 imam atthaṃ dhaniyo abhāsatha     sn i         
      lābhā   vata no anappakā    
 ye mayaṃ bhagavantaṃ addasāma  
 saraṇaṃ taṃ upema cakkhuma  
 satthā no hohi tuvam   mahāmuni     sn i         
     gopī ca ahañ ca assava 
 brahmacariyaṃ sugate carāmase    
 jātimaraṇassa   pāragā   
 dukkhass  antakarā bhavāmase      sn i

   uragavagga 
      nandati puttehi puttimā  
 iti māro pāpimā 
 gomiko  gohi tath  eva nandati  
 upadhī hi narassa nandanā  
 na hi so nandati yo nirūpadhi       sn i         
      socati puttehi puttimā  
 iti bhagavā

    khaggavisāṇasutta  
  f         sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ 
 aviheṭhayaṃ aññataram pi tesaṃ 
 na puttam iccheyya kuto sahāyaṃ  
 eko care khaggavisāṇakappo     sn i        
     saṃsaggajātassa bhavati sneho   
 snehanvayaṃ dukkham idam  pahoti  
 ādīnavaṃ snehajaṃ pekkhamāno 
 eko care khaggavisāṇakappo     sn i        
     mitte suhajje anukampamāno 
 hāpeti atthaṃ paṭibaddhacitto   
 etaṃ bhayaṃ santhave pekkhamāno 
 eko care khaggavisāṇakappo     sn i        
     vaṃso visālo va  yathā visatto 
 puttesu dāresu ca yā apekhā

 saṃsīnapatto   yathā koviḷāro

     sīho va saddesu asantasanto 
 vāto va jālamhi asajjamāno 
 padumaṃ va toyena alippamāno  
 eko care          sn i         
     sīho yathā dāṭhabalī pasayha

     mettaṃ upekhaṃ karuṇaṃ vimuttiṃ

    parābhavasutta  
 evam me sutaṃ  
 ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane 
 anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme  atha kho aññatarā devatā

 ajjhabhāsi

  f         vasalasutta   
 evam me sutaṃ  
 ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane 
 anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme  atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaraṃ  ādāya sāvatthiṃ  piṇḍāya 
 pāvisi  tena kho pana samayena aggikabhāradvājassa 
 brāhmaṇassa nivesane aggi pajjalito hoti  āhutī  paggahitā  
 atha kho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ sapasānaṃ piṇḍāya 
 caramāno yena aggikaghāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ ten  upasaṃkami  addasā kho aggikabhāradvājo 
 brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ dūrato va āgacchantaṃ  disvāna 
 bhagavantaṃ etad avoca   tatr  eva  muṇḍaka  tatr  eva  
 samanaka  tatr  eva  vasalaka tiṭṭhāhī  ti  evaṃ vutte 
 bhagavā aggikabhāradvājaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etad avoca  
  jānāsi pana tvaṃ brāhmaṇa vasalaṃ vā  vasalakaraṇe vā 
 dhamme  ti   na khv āhaṃ bho gotama jānami vasalaṃ 
 vā vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme  sādhu me bhavaṃ gotamo  
 tathā dhammaṃ desetu  yathāhaṃ jāneyyaṃ vasalaṃ vā 
 vasalakaraṇe vā dhamme  ti   tena hi brāhmaṇa 
 suṇāhi  sādhukaṃ manasikarohi  bhāsissāmī  ti   evam  
 bho  ti kho aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavato 
 paccassosi  bhagavā etad avoca

    mahāmaṅgalasutta   
 evam me sutaṃ  
 ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane 
 anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme  atha kho aññatarā devatā 
 abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā ten  upasaṃkami  upasaṃkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi  
 ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya 
 ajjhabhāsi  
       bahū devā manussā ca maṅgalāni acintayuṃ 
 ākaṃkhamānā sotthānaṃ  brūhi maṅgalam uttamaṃ      sn ii        
       asevanā ca bālānaṃ paṇḍitānañ ca sevanā 
 pūjā ca pūjanīyānaṃ   etam  maṅgalam uttamaṃ     sn ii

 attasammāpaṇidhi ca  etam  maṅgalam uttamaṃ     sn ii

    nāvāsutta   
      yasmā  hi dhammaṃ puriso  vijaññā   
 indaṃ va naṃ devatā pūjayeyya  
 so pūjito tasmiṃ  pasannacitto 
 bahussuto pātukaroti dhammaṃ     sn ii        
      tad aṭṭhikatvāna nisamma dhīro 
 dhammānudhammaṃ paṭipajjamāno 
 viññū vibhāvī  nipuṇo ca hoti  
 yo tādisaṃ bhajati  appamatto     sn ii        
      khuddañ ca bālaṃ upasevamāno 
 anāgatatthañ ca bālaṃ usūyakañ  ca 
 idh  eva dhammaṃ avibhāvayitvā 
 avitiṇṇakaṃkho maraṇaṃ upeti     sn ii        
      yathā naro āpagaṃ  otaritvā 
 mahodikaṃ salilaṃ   sīghasotaṃ

 kiṃ so pare sakkhati tārayetuṃ     sn ii

 kiṃ so pare sakkhati nijjhapetuṃ       sn ii

    subhāsitasutta   
 evam me sutaṃ  
 ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane 
   pe     bhagavā etad avoca   catūhi  bhikkhave aṅgehi 
 samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti na  dubbhāsitā anavajjā 
 ca ananuvajjā  ca viññūnaṃ  katamehi catūhi   idha 
 bhikkhave  bhikkhu subhāsitañ ñeva  bhāsati no dubbhāsitaṃ  dhammañ ñeva  bhāsati no adhammaṃ  piyañ ñeva  
 bhāsati no appiyaṃ  saccañ ñeva  bhāsati no alikaṃ   
 imehi kho bhikkhave catūhi  aṅgehi samannāgatā vācā  
 subbāsitā hoti na  dubbhāsitā anavajjā ca ananuvajjā  ca

  f          vāseṭṭhadutta   
 evam me sutaṃ  
 ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā icchānaṃkale  viharati icchānaṃkalavanasaṇḍe  tena kho pana samayena sambahulā

 todeyyabrāhmaṇo  aññe ca abhiññātā abhiññātā  brāhmaṇamahāsālā  atha kho vāseṭṭha bhāradvājānaṃ māṇavānaṃ  jaṃghāvihāraṃ   anucaṃkamamānānaṃ   anuvicaramānānaṃ   ayam antarākathā udapādi   kathaṃ 
 bho brāhmaṇo hotī  ti    bhāradvājo māṇavo evam āha  
  yato kho bho   ubhato sujāto hoti mātito ca pitito ca 
 saṃsuddhagahaṇiko yāva sattamā pitāmahayugā   akkhitto

 sīlavā ca hoti vatasampanno   ca    ettāvatā kho   brāhmaṇo hotī  ti  n  eva kho asakkhi bhāradvājo māṇavo

 bhagavantaṃ etad avoca   kīvadīghaṃ nu kho bhante 
 padume niraye  āyuppamāṇan  ti   dīghaṃ kho bhikkhu 
 padume niraye  āyuppamāṇaṃ  taṃ na sukaraṃ  saṃkhātuṃ  ettakāni vassāni  iti vā  ettakāni vassasatāni

    kāmasutta  
      kāmaṃ kāmayamānassa tassa ce taṃ samijjhati  
 addhā  pītimano hoti laddhā macco yad icchati      sn iv        
      tassa ce kāmayānassa  chandajātassa jantuno 
 te kāmā parihāyanti  sallaviddho va ruppati     sn iv        
      yo kāme parivajjeti sappasseva padā siro  
 so imaṃ  visattikaṃ loke sato samativattati      sn iv        
      khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraññaṃ vā gavāssaṃ  dāsaporisaṃ  
 thiyo  bandhū puthu kāme yo naro anugijjhati     sn iv        
      abalā va  naṃ balīyanti  maddante naṃ parissayā  
 tato naṃ dukkham anveti nāvaṃ bhinnam ivodakaṃ     sn iv        
      tasmā jantu sadā sato kāmāni parivajjaye  
 te pahāya tare oghaṃ nāvaṃ siñcitvā   pāragū ti    sn iv        
 kāmasuttaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ
